ENTRY       EC 5.99.1.3                 Enzyme
NAME        DNA topoisomerase (ATP-hydrolysing);
            type II DNA topoisomerase;
            DNA-gyrase;
            deoxyribonucleate topoisomerase;
            deoxyribonucleic topoisomerase;
            topoisomerase;
            DNA topoisomerase II
CLASS       Isomerases;
            Other isomerases;
            Sole sub-subclass for isomerases that do not belong in the other subclasses
SYSNAME     DNA topoisomerase (ATP-hydrolysing)
REACTION    ATP-dependent breakage, passage and rejoining of double-stranded DNA
COMMENT     The enzyme can introduce negative superhelical turns into double-stranded circular DNA. One unit has nicking-closing activity, and another catalyses super-twisting and hydrolysis of ATP (cf. EC 5.99.1.2 DNA topoisomerase).
HISTORY     EC 5.99.1.3 created 1984
REFERENCE   1  [PMID:6267993]
  AUTHORS   Gellert M.
  TITLE     DNA topoisomerases.
  JOURNAL   Annu. Rev. Biochem. 50 (1981) 879-910.
ORTHOLOGY   K02469  DNA gyrase subunit A
            K02470  DNA gyrase subunit B
            K03164  DNA topoisomerase II
            K03166  DNA topoisomerase VI subunit A
            K03167  DNA topoisomerase VI subunit B
            K03170  reverse gyrase
